No cheats!\r\n- Customize your game by choosing the number of opponents, cards in the stockpile and  game difficulty.\r\n- Play online together with friends or family everywhere: Smartphone, PC or Mac.\r\n- Chat with online opponents\r\n- Unlimited undo\r\n- Scoreboard with player rankings\r\n- Resume games after pause\r\n- Help for the beginners\r\n- No frills.\r\n- Browser game at https://skipoid-nexus.appspot.com for PC or Mac.\r\n\r\nGame rules:\r\n\r\nThe object of the game is to be the first player to play out their entire stock pile. \r\nEach player is dealt 10 (20 or 30) cards for their stock pile with only the uppermost card visible, and a hand of five card. \r\nThe shared play area allows up to four build piles, which must be started using either a \"1\" card or a '*', and each player also has up to four personal discard piles. \r\nEach turn the active player draws until he has five cards in hand, and plays on the build piles. He must play either the next card in sequential order or a wild '*' card, using either cards in hand, the top card of his stock pile, or the top card of any of his four discard piles. If the player can play all five cards from hand, he draws five more and continues playing. When no more plays are available, the player discards one card to either an empty discard pile or on top of an existing one and play passes to the next player. When a build pile reaches 12, it is removed from the board and that space becomes empty for another pile to be started; play continues until one player has played his final start
